new entry "Interrupt_EmpoweredStrike_Amplified"
type "InterruptData"
data "DisplayName" "1C7FD0B67E9E24A0F64B1288B574D23B0F014"
data "Description" "6ECBEA0DB51EA81DADB151E8F46B305ED91FB"
data "Icon" "PsionicTalent_Psion_EmpoweredStrike"
data "InterruptContext" "OnCastHit"
data "InterruptContextScope" "Self"
